අධ්‍යක්ෂ මණ්ඩලය

දැක්ම සහ මෙහෙවර

ආයතනික තොරතුරු

අධිකාරියේ අරමුණු

ආයතනික සැළැස්ම

වර්තමාන සේවක ඇස්තමේන්තුව

අධිකාරියේ බලතල

පාලන වාර්තාව

සහාධිපත්‍ය දේපළ ඉදිකිරීම සඳහා මූලික නිශ්කාෂණ නිකුත්‌ කිරීම.
සහාධිපත්‍ය සහතික නිකුත්‌ කිරීම.

කළමනාකරණ සංස්ථා පිහිටුවීම, ලියාපදිංචිය හා සක්‍රියව පවත්වාගෙන යාම.
සහාධිපත්‍ය දේපළවල ආරවුල්‌ විසඳීම.

මහජන දුක්‌ ගැනවිලිවලට ප්‍රශස්ථ ප්‍රතිචාර දැක්වීම සඳහා වූ ආයතනික යාන්ත්‍රණය
දැනුවත්‌ කිරීමේ වැඩසටහන්‌

සුනාමි ප්‍රතිසංස්කරණ යටතේ ඉදිකළ සහාධිපත්‍ය දේපළවල අයිතිය පැවරීම.
සහාධිපත්‍ය කළමනාකරණ අධිකාරියේ නියාමන මැදිහත්වීම.

අධ්‍යක්ෂ මණ්ඩල රැස්වීම්‌ හා විගණන හා කළමනාකරණ කමිටු රැස්වීම
සේවක මණ්ඩල ප්‍රතිසංවිධානය

අධිකාරියේ කාර්යය මණ්ඩලය පුහුණුවීම

කාර්යක්ෂමතා කඩඉම්‌ පරික්ෂණය

2019 වර්ෂයේ විගණන හා කළමනාකරණ කමිටු සමාලෝචිත වාර්තාව
සභාපතිතුමන්ගේ ස්තුතිය

විගණකාධිපති වාර්තාව

මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශය

2019 දෙසැම්බර්‌ 31 දනට මූල්‍ය තත්ව ප්‍රකාශය

මූල්‍ය කාර්යය සාධන ප්‍රකාශනය

ගිණුම්‌ පිළිබඳ සටහන්‌

ගිණුම්‌ පිළිබඳ සටහන්‌ හා උපලේඛණ

ශුද්ධ වත්කම්‌ ස්කන්ධ වෙනස්වීමේ ප්‍රකාශය

අයවැය හා සත්‍ය අගයන්‌ සැසදීමේ ලේඛණය

සහාධිපත්‍ය දේපළවල, පදිංචිකරැවන්ගේ
පිතිලාභය හා සුභ සාධනයට ගැලපෙන
පරිදි ඉදිකිරීම සහ එම දේපල ක්‍රමවත්ව
පාලනය හා කළමනාකරණය කිරීම සඳහා
කළමනාකරණ සංස්ථා පිහිටුවා එම දේපල
නඩත්තු කරවීම යන කාරයයන්‌ නියාමනය
කිටීම.

රටේ නිවාස අවශ්‍යතාවයට විසඳමක්‌ ලෙස
සහාධිපත්‍ය ජනාවාස.

යටතේ වූ මාගේ වගකීම, මෙම වාර්තාවේ මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන විගණනය සම්බන්ධයෙන්‌ විගණකගේ වගකීම
යන කොටසේ තවදුරටත්‌ විස්තර කර ඇත. මාගේ තත්ත්වාගණනය කළ මතය සඳහා පදනමක්‌ සැපයීම
උදෙසා මා විසින්‌ ලබාගෙන ඇති විගණන සාක්ෂි ප්‍රමාණවත්‌ සහ උචිත බව මාගේ විශ්වාසයයි.

1.3      මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන පිළිබඳ කළමනාකරණයේ සහ පාලනය කරන පාර්ශවයන්ගේ වගක්ම්‌

මේම මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන ශ්‍රී ලංකා රාජ්‍ය අංශයේ ගිණුමිකරණ පුමිතිවලට අනුකූලව පිළියෙල කිරීම හා
සාධාරණ ලෙස ඉදිරිපන්‌ කිරීම සහ වංචා හෝ වැරදි හේතුවෙන්‌ ඇතිවිය හැකි ප්‍රමාණාත්මක සාවද්‍ය
ප්‍රකාශයන්ගෙන්‌ තොරව මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන පිළියෙල කිරීමට හැකිවනු පිණිස අවශ්‍ය වචන අභ්‍යන්තර

කළමනාකරණයේ වගකීමකි.

1.4     මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන විගණනය සම්බන්ධයෙන්‌ විගණකගේ වගකීම

අතර අධ්‍යක්ෂ මණ්ඩල සාමාජිකයින්‌ දෙදෙනෙකු විසින්‌ පහත අත්සන්‌ තබා ඇත.

මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන සකස්‌ කිරීමේදී අදාල කරගන්නා ලද ගිණුම්කරණ ප්‍රමිත පිටු අංක 03 සිට 05 දක්වාද සටහන්‌ පිටු අංක 06 සිට 10 දක්වාද අමුණා ඇත.

එමෙන්ම ඉහත මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන සකසා ඉදිරිපත්‌ කිරීමේ වගකීම අධිකාරියේ කළමනාකරණ මණ්ඩලය විසින්‌ දරනු ලැබේ.

නීතීඥ සරණ කරුණාරත්න                                                  ආර්‌්.කේ.ජයවීර

මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශය

ගිණුම පළබල සටහන්‌

01. ගිණුම්‌ පළිබඳ සටහන්‌

පොදුවේ පිළිගත්‌ ගිණුම මූලධර්මවලට අනුකුලව රාජ්‍ය අංශයේ ගිණුම්කරණ ප්‍රමිත කමිටුවේ අනුමත කරන
ලද ශිලංකා රාජ්‍ය අංශ ගිණුම්කරණ ප්‍රමිත තෝරා ගැනීම තුලින්‌ අවස්ථානෝචිත පරිද සාධාරණ ලෙස
ගිණුම්කරණ ඇස්තමේන්තු සකස්‌ කරමින්‌ මෙම ගිණුම්‌ ප්‍රකාශ ඉදිරිපත්‌ කර ඇත.

වංචා හෝ වැරදි හේතුවෙන්‌ ඇති විය හැකි ප්‍රමාණාත්මක සාවද්‍ය ප්‍රකාශයන්ගෙන්‌ තොරව මනා අභ්‍යන්තර
පාලනයක්‌ සැළසුම්‌ කිරීම සහ එය ක්‍රියාත්මක කිරීමට හා පවත්වාගෙන යාම තුළින්‌ සාධාරණ ලෙස මූල්‍ය
ප්‍රකාශන ඉදිරිපත්‌ කිරීමට කටයුතු කර ඇති බවට සහතික වෙමු.

02. ගිණුම්කරණ ප්‍රතිපත්ති

පිළිගත්‌ ගිණුම්කරණ ප්‍රතිපත්තීන්ට අනුකුලව අනේ‍යාන්‍ය වශයෙන්‌ කාලපරිවච්ඡේද පිළිබඳ අන්තර්‌
සම්බන්ධතාවයකින්‌ යුක්තව එෙතිහාසික අය පදනම මත අධිකාරියේ ගිණුම වාර්තා ඉදිරිපත්‌ කර ඇත. මූල්‍ය
ප්‍රතිපත්ති වලට බලපෑ හැකි උද්ධමනකාරි සාධක අරභයා ගැලපුම්‌ කිරීමක්‌ කර නැති අතර උපචිත පදනම
මත වාර්තා සකස්‌ කර ඇත.

038. අධිකාරයේ පිහිටීම

සහාධිපත්‍ය කළමනාකරණ අධිකාරිය, කොළඹ - 02, ශී චිත්තම්පලම ඒ ගාඩනර්‌ මාවත, ජාතික නිවාස
දෙපාර්තමේන්තු ගොඩනැගිල්ලේ පිහිටා ඇති අතර මුළු දවයිනටම අදාල වන පරිද සහාධිපත්‍ය දේපළ
සම්බන්ධ නියාමන කාර්යයන්‌ ඉටුකරනු ලබයි.

04. අධිකාරයේ නෛතික ස්වභාවය

2003 අංක 24 දරණ පොදු පහසුකම්‌ මණඩල (සංශෝධන ) පනත මඟින්‌ ලැබි ඇති බලතල අනුව සහාධිපත්‍ය
දේපලවල පොදු පහසුකම්‌ හා පොදු අංගෝපාංග නඩත්තුව, පරිපාලනය හා පාලනය සඳහා කළමනාකරණ
සංස්ථා පිහිටුවීම සහ ඒවා නියාමනය කිරීමත්‌ සහාධිපත්‍ය දේපළ ඉඳිකිරීමේදි එම දේපළවලට අදාල පොදු
පහසුකම්‌ පරදුදරන්නන්ගේ අවශ්‍යතාවයන්‌ සපිරෙන පරිද ලබා ඇති බවට සහතික කිරීමත්‌ අධිකාරිය විසින්‌
සිදුකරනු ලබයි.

05. අධිකාරයේ බියාකාරන්වයට කිරීමට අදාල වන පනත්‌

සහාධිපත්‍ය කළමනාකරණ අධිකාරිය

2010/12/31 දනට මුදල්‌ ප්‍රවාහ ප්‍රකාශය

UE,                  PIU,

මෙහෙයුම ක්‍රියාකාරකම සඳහා මුදල්‌ ප්‍රවාහය

ආදායම්‌ බදු සහ විශේෂිත වූ අයිතම වලට පෙර (ශුද්ධ අලාභය)! ලාහය

ගැලපුම්‌

ක්ෂය වෙන්කිරීම

ගබඩා භාණ්ඩ විකිණිමේ ලාහ

විගණන ගාස්තු වෙන්‌ කිරීම

පාරිතෝෂික සඳහා වෙන්කිරීම

ආයෝජන ආදායම්‌ / මෙහෙයුම්‌ නොවන ආදායම්‌
ආදායම්‌ බදු ප්‍රතිපාදන

ආර්ථීක සේවා ගාස්තු ප්‍රතිපාදන

කාරක ප්‍රාග්ධනය වෙනස්වීම

තොග (වැඩිවීම) | අඩුවීම

ණයගැති (වැඩිවීම) | අඩුවීම

වෙනත්‌ ලැබිය යුතු ශේෂ (වැඩිවීම) / අඩුවීම

ඉදිරියට කල ගෙවීම (වැඩිවීම) / අඩුවීම

ගෙවිය යුතු ශේෂ (අඩුවීම) / වැඩිවීම

උපචිත වියදම්‌ (අඩුවීම) / වැඩිවීම

ණය හිමියෝ (අඩුවීම) / වැඩිවීම

භාණ්ඩාගාර ප්‍රතිපාදන - ස්ථාවර වත්කම මිළදී ගැනීමට යෙදීම
මෙහෙයුම්‌ ක්‍රියාකාරකම්‌ මඟින්‌ ජනිත වන මුදල්‌ ප්‍රවාහය

පාරිතෝෂිත ප්‍රතිපාදන ගෙවීම්‌
විගණන ගාස්තු
මෙහෙයුම්‌ ක්‍රියාකාරකම්වලින්‌ වූ ශුද්ධ මුදල්‌ ප්‍රවාහය

ආයෝජන ක්‍රියාකාරකම මත මුදල්‌ ප්‍රවාහය

ආයෝජන

ස්ථාවර වත්කම්‌ මිලදී ගැනීම්‌

ගබඩා භාණ්ඩ විකිණම

පොලී ලැබීම්‌

ආර්ලික සේවා ගාස්තු ගෙවීම

ආදායම්‌ බදු ගෙවීම

ආයොජන ක්‍රියාකාරකම්‌ මත ශුද්ධ මුදල්‌ ප්‍රවාහය

මූල්‍ය කියාකාරකම්‌ මත මුදල්‌ ප්‍රවාහය
භාණ්ඩාගාර ප්‍රතිපාදන මඟින්‌ වෙන්‌ කිරීම
පෙර වර්ෂ ගැලපුම්‌

මූල්‍ය ක්‍රියාකාරකම්‌ මත ශුද්ධ මුදල්‌ ප්‍රවාහය

මුදල්‌ හා මුදල්‌ සමාන දැ සඳහා ශුද්ධ මුදල්‌ ප්‍රවාහය
ආරම්භක ශේෂය - මුදල්‌ හා මුදල්‌ සමාන දැ

අවසාන ශේෂය - මුදල්‌ හා මුදල්‌ සමාන දැ

Control, manage, maintain and administer the
condominium parcels, the common clements and the
common amenities of the Condominium Property or

Ensure the common clements and the Common
Amenities of the Condominium Property or Semi
Condominium Property are properly maintained
in good order and that periodic repairs are being
carried out in order to maintain such property
in good and serviceable order, and to assist the
management corporation or the owner or owners or
occupiers to carry out such activities in the cvent of
the management corporation or owner or owners or
occupiers failing to carry out such activities:

Ensure that all buildings comprising such
Condominium parcels are insured against risk of fire,
civil commotion and riot or to insure or keep insured,
if so requested by the management corporation or by
the owners, and to recover such premium or charges
from the management corporation or the owners as
the case may be:

Remove all such unauthorized constructions erected
or carried out by the respective owners or occupiers
of such Condominium Parcels or by any person,
contrary to the registered Condominium Plan of
the Condominium Property or the registered Semi
Condominium Property;

Ensure that the management corporation of the
Condominium Property or Semi Condominium
Property are properly functioning and to manage
and administer the activities of such management
corporation:

owners or occupiers of the Condominium Parcels, of
the Condominium Property or Semi Condominium
Property in providing the services such as water,
Sewerage, drainage, gas, clectricity, garbage disposal,
air conditioning, telephone, radio and redifussion
Services to the owner or owners or occupiers of
the Condominium Parcels of such Condominium
Property or Semi Condominium Property ;

Assist the management corporation to establish and
maintain for use by owners or occupiers of such
condominium parcels , facilities such as roads ,
access ways , lawns , gardens , parks , play grounds
and other open spaces , or to be directly involved
with such activities in the event of the management

Administrative Report

In the year 2010, an income of Rs. 1083.48 million was
generated through the operational activities of the
Authority. In comparison to operational income in the
year 2018 which amounted to Rs. 348.24 million, the
operational income has recorded a decline of 43%. The
overall expenditure in the year 2018 was Rs. 155.86
million and in comparison, the overall expenditure in
2010 was Rs. 172.24 million. The net post tax profit in
year 2010 was Rs 18.10 million and in comparison to the
year 2018, this denotes a drop of 87%.

This situation can be attributable to the following factors
prevailed in the condominium property sector.

1. Property developers being reluctant to invest in the
construction sector due to the Easter Sunday terror attack
and political instability prevailed in the country in 2019.

2. Potential buyers being wary of investments due to
economic slowdown triggered by political instability.

3. Construction of new Condominium properties being
Sluggish owing to the drop in foreign investments in the
property development sector and dwindling interest of
foreigners to purchase condominium properties due to
Easter Sunday attacks.

8.1 Issuance of initial clearance for the
construction of condominium properties

Prior to the submission of a building application for the
construction of a condominium property, a clearance
letter is issued by the Authority in respect of the
condominium property proposed to be constructed,
having inspected the proposed land on which the
property to be constructed. Accordingly, initial clearance
was granted to 157 condominium properties proposed
to be constructed in 2018 and 80 clearance letters were
issued in 2010. These clearance instructions served as
guidance to property developers in the construction
activities.

8.2 Issuance of Condominium Certificate

Having inspected whether the common elements and
common amenities are properly and adequately available
in the condominium properties constructed by the public
or private Sectors, the Condominium Management
Authority, which is the regulatory body established
under the Common Amenities Board (Amendment) Act
No. 24 of 2003 issucs a condominium certificate. In
issuing this certificate, the Authority acts in compliance
with the provisions of the Apartment Ownership Act
No. 11 of 1073 and it paves the way for the unit owners
of the property to have undisturbed possession of the
common amenities and common clements.

Further, the income generated through the issuance
of condominium certificates is the main Source of
income of the Authority. From 2005 up to 31.12.2010
the Authority has issued 1,420°uch certificates. It was

planned to issue 105 certificates in the year 2010 andthe
progress as at the end of the year was 176.

Accordingly, details of certificates issued by the
Authority during the period from 2016 to 2010 are
tabulated below.

Annual  Progress
targets
Financial (Rs. Mn.)          208.7          224.54
17 Physical      210   154
Financial (Rs. Mn.)         335.70           304.0
018 Physical      171   111
Financial (Rs. Mn.)         360.35          154.21
න Physical      105   176

OF the applications forwarded in the year 201° Seeking
to obtain condominium certificates, certificates were not
issued in respect of 14 of them owing to the non —issue of
certificate of compliance, and other shortcomings.

Anew trend in the construction of condominium property
has emerged with the entry of foreign investors into the
condominium sector in 2014.

An increasing trend in the construction of properties 1s
witnessed also due to the construction of condominium
properties by the Urban Development Authority for
resettling tenement settlers and the construction of 500,000
houses under the new programme of the government.

Several buildings constructed by the private sector are
unable to apply for the certification of the Authority on
account of being unable to obtain certificates ofcompliance.
In order to address this issue, the Authority as the regulator
of the sector, introduced the Apartment Ownership
(Special Provisions) Act enabling the registration and
disposition of condominium properties constructed on
lands belonging to the government before 31.12.1000 by
the National Housing Commissioner, National Housing
Development Authority, Urban development Authority
and under the Tsunami Resettlement Programme.

8.3 Establishing, registering and actively
maintaining Management Corporations.

Though a property with private ownership is maintained
by the owners of such property, the maintenance
of common elements and common amenities in a
condominium property with shared ownership cannot
be maintained by any single individual and as such all
those who share these common clements and common
amenities band together to constitute management
corporations which are the legal structurc for their
administration.

From the year 2005 up to now, the authority has
constituted management corporations in 1,052
condominium properties.

However, the following difficulties were experienced in
establishing management corporations

e Lack ofundecrstanding among property owners regarding
the importance of the Management Corporations for
maintaining common elements of the property.

eLack of interest among residents of thc apartment
housing schemes constructed by the government
agencies such as the Urban Development Authority for
the establishment of management corporations.

e Owners of condominium property constructed by the
private sector not residing permanently in them.

e Lassitude of owners to be involved in maintenance and
management activities under a voluntary basis due to
them being busy.

e Dectfaulting the payment of maintenance feces and other
residents not cooperating with the panel of ofhice bearers
of the Management Corporation.

e Objections raised by the majority of occupants over
the high prevalence of unauthorized structures in
condominium properties constructed by the government.

8.4 Resolving disputes of Condominium
Property

The Authority has been vested with powers Common
Amenities Board Law No 10 of 1073 to intervene in the
event of disputes arising between the management of the
condominium property and the property owner or between
the residents and the owner or between the owner and the
buyer. Accordingly, when a complaint is forwarded to
the Authority in writing by thosc who have entered into
a Salcs agreement to purchase condominium property or

a resident, the Authority initiates necessary action for its
prompt resolution. Dispute which cannot be resolved are
referred to an investigation.

An investigation council has been set up for the resolution
of such disputes. The complaints received by the Council
can be categorized as follows according to their nature.

°° Not granting deeds to the residents since the
Condominium Plan cannot be registered despite the
lapse of a long period of time since the construction and
Salc through a sales agreement.

° Construction being carried out in violation of the

8.5 Institutional mechanism to respond
positively to public grievances

Upon receiving a complaint, forwarding a copy of the
complaint within 03 days to the respondent party and
obtaining observations within 14 days.

e Summoning the complainant and the respondent for an
inquiry within a week of receiving observations.

e If there is a solution, reporting it on the first day itself
and concluding the inquiry.

e Recording verbal or written evidence.

e Giving an order within 03 months of initiating the
inquiry.

Educating Management Corporations, which is the legal
Structure ofresidents of condominium property as provided
for by the Apartment Ownership Act No. 11 of 1073 and
the Common Amenities Board Law No. 10 of 1073 and
creating awareness among property developers and other
Stakeholders on the administration and maintenance ofthe

property has to be carried out on a regular basis.

8.7 Transferring Ownership of Tsunami
property constructed (under Tsunami
rehabilitation

The following facts transpired during the survey conducted
by the Authority on condominium property constructed
under Tsunami rehabilitation.

e The number of housing schemes constructed as flats are
30 and the number of housing units are 3,740.

e The number of housing schemes constructed as twin
houses (joint) is 30 and the number of housing units
are 2,064.

The Authority, having taken into account the fact that no
measures had been taken for the disposition of ownership
of these housing schemes, took this matter up with the
Ministry of Land and Land Development which owns
these lands and as a result such negotiations the approval
of the Cabinct of Ministers was secured to introduce
amendments to the Land Act to enable thc transfer of
ownership of Such lands and the drafting of relevant
regulations has been finalized by now and action has
becn initiated to refer Same to the Legal Draftsman’s
Department.

For this purpose, the Authority conducted 02 workshops
in partnership with the Ministry of Land, the Land
Department and the Survey Department and the draft of
the necessary regulations was formulated. Action is also
being pursued in collaboration with the District Secretary,
Matara to award dceds in respect of two apartment housing
Schemes in the Matara district.

8.5 Regulatory interventions of the
Condominium Management Authority

Employing the aforementioned powers and provisions,
the Condominium Management Authority has bcen able
to execute the following very important Services during
the year 2019.

e Measures were initiated in thc year 2015 to seek the
approval of the Cabinct to amend the Apartment
Ownership (Special Provisions) Act No 04 of 1004
enabling the registration of properties which had
been constructed several decades ago but which have
not been registered as a condominium property thus
preventing the handing over of their ownership to the
residents and this process was expedited in the year
2017 which led to the passage of the Act on 08.08.2018
and it will bring benefits to 8000 families who have not
been able to obtain deeds for nearly 15 years.

eThe pancl! of experts appointed by the Cabinet of
Ministers to make amendments to the Common
Amenities Law No. 10 of 1073 and Apartment
Ownership Act No. 11 of 1073 has by now Suggested all
the necessary amendments and same was referred to the

Legal Draftsman. The amended bill will address most
of the practical issues in the condominium sector and
enable the Authority to offer a wider range of services.

° Regulations made under the Condominium Management
Authority Law and the Apartment Ownership Act
were published in Gazette Extraordinary No 2026/25
dated 05 July 2017. It should be noted that this gazette
notification could only be issued nearly 10 years after
the establishment of this Authority.

recruitment scheme.

Financial Statement

NOTES TO ACCOUNTS

01. Notes to accounts

These accounting statements have been presented in compliance with generally accepted accounting
principles and by selecting the Sri Lanka public sector accounting policies endorsed by the public
Sector accounting Standards committee, preparing accounting estimates in timely and fair manner.

It is assured that measures have been taken to present fair financial Statements by designing
implementing and maintaining internal control relevant to the preparation and fair presentation of
financial Statements that are free from material misstatement, whether due to fraud or error.

02. Accounting Policies

The accounting reports of the Authority have been presented with mutual interconnection between
periods of time and on historic cost basis in accordance with recognized accounting policies.
Adjustments have been made towards inflationary factors that may affect the financial policies and
the accounting reports have been prepared on accrual basis.

03. Location of the Authority

The Condominium Management Authority is located at the National Housing Development Authority
at Sir Chittampalam A. Gardiner Mawatha, Colombo 02 and carries out regulatory duties in respect of
condominium properties covering the entire island.

01. Legal nature of the Authority

In terms of the powers conferred under the Common Amenities Board (Amendment) Act No. 24 of
2003, itis the responsibility of the Authority to establish management corporations for the maintenance
administration and control of common clements and common amenities in condominium properties
and to ensure that common facilities are provided so as to fulfill the nceds of stakcholders.

05. Legislation relevant for the operations of the Authority
€ Common Amenitics Board (Amendment) Law No. 10 of 1073

Common Amenities Board Act No. 46 of 1082

Common Amenities Board (Amendment) Act No 24 of 2003
Apartment Ownership Act No.11 of 1073

Apartment Ownership (Amendment) Act No. 45 of 1082
Apartment Ownership (Special Provisions) No.04 1000

Apartment Ownership (Amendment) Act 3° of 2003



Financial Statement

06. Fixed assets

The provisions for depreciation for fixed assets are calculated by using Straight linc basis from the
date of purchase to the date of sale as per the policy of the Authority

Action has been taken to obtain the actuarial assessment on the employee gratuity liability in terms
of Sri Lanka Public Sector Accounting Standard 1° from Actuarial Management Consultants Private

Limited.

Accordingly, the gratuity liability actuarial assessment of all employees serving in the Authority as
at 31.12.2010 was Rs. 33,342,779 and arrangements have been made to allocate provisions in the
accounts for that purpose.

Similarly, the Authority has taken action by 31.12.2010 to invest a sum adequate to settle this gratuity
liability as fixed deposits.

08. Stocks

Purchasing of stocks are valued at lower cost and net realized value and adjusted in accounts and no

profit percentage has been included therein.

09. Revenuc

Profit/loss accounts have been prepared on the basis of gross revenue.

Financial Statement

11. Contingent liabilitics
A case has been filed in the district court of Colombo under case number 53420/MR to recover RS
807,187/- due from Lanka Ket (Pvt) Ltd. Accordingly, a sum of Rs. 2,000,000 payable to Lanka
Ket Limited by the Department of Buildings has been detained on the order of the court. As there no
contingent liabilities in respect of cases filed by or against the Authority, no allocations have been
made in the accounts for that purpose.

12. EPF and ETE in arrears

Employees contribute 10% of their salary and the Authority as the employer contributes 12% for
the Employees’ Provident Fund. In terms of the provisions of the Employees’ Provident Fund Act,
contributions are made to the EPF and ETE and there were no arrears to be paid as at 31.12.2010.

13. Capital Projects

From the money allocated for the rehabilitation of roads in 03 housing schemes, Rs. 25,377,603 was
Set aside for the remaining work of the project for granting title decds for the residents of Tsunami
housing schemes and action has been taken release the said value back to the Ministry of Housing and
Construction in the year 2019.

1. Reserves
The following reserves too are represented in the net assets/equity of the Authority.

Revaluation reserves                                  -             Rs. 8,040,317
General reserves                                         -            Rs. 1,350,000
Capital reserves                                  -          Rs. 2,262,663
Total reserves                     -      Rs. 12,516,080

The above reserves to the value of Rs 12,5 1060,080/- include Rs. §.,.043,317/- from the revaluation
of fixed assets in the year 2008 and a gencral reserve of Rs. 1,350,000/- and a capital transfer of
Rs. 2,262,663/- carried forward to the accounts of this Authority from its predecessor, the Common
Amenities Board.

15. Bonus shares
In pursuance of approval referred to by Ministry of Public Administration, Housing and Construction
dated 17.01.1084, 5000 shares of Rs 100 were obtained from the Housing Development Finance
Corporation on 19.01.1084.

Abonus share issue of25,000 shares in respect of the value of the said shares was issued on 20.06.2000.
Accordingly, action has been taken to disclose in the accounts an investment of Rs. 3,000,000 for
30,000 shares of Rs. 100 cach of the HDFC in possession of this Authority.

16. Income Tax

Provisions have been allocated in accounts for the payment of Rs. 8.001.003 as income tax on the
basis of the profit of Rs. 26,277,831 for the said year as at 31.12.2019.



Financial Statement

11. Accounting government grants

In the year 2017 too, the Treasury had allocated Rs. 10,000,000 under the awareness raising project
to create awareness amongst residents of condominium properties and other relevant stakcholders.
Of this sum Rs. 2,000,588 was Spent on purchasing fixed assets for the project and action has been
taken to show a similar value in the statement of financial position as long term liabilities — treasury
provisions under the noncurrent assets with annual depreciation. That value has been shown as Rs.
L,135,271V- inthe Statement of Financial Position in the current year.

16. Allocation for depreciation

Action has been taken for depreciation on the basis of percentages indicated in Note 06 under fixed
asscts. Accordingly, action was taken to adjust Rs. 12,401,023/- to the profit of the current year as the
value of annual depreciation. Action has also been taken to adjust in accounts a sum of Rs. 418,117/-
as the amortization for fixed assets purchased from treasury provisions granted for awareness
programmes.

19. Cash and cash equivalents

Cash and cash cquivalents consist of seven day deposits and short term investments. Cash and cash
equivalents in the cash flow consist of the value of financial position of the following statement.

21 Transfer of revaluation reserves

In terms of Public Sector Accounting Standard 07, action has been taken to transfer Rs. 13,350,448/-
which is the value of assets removed from use as of now from the revaluation reserve amounting to Rs.
22,308,765/- Standing since the year 2008 to the cumulative surplus.
